4. # **Final Product Requirements** {#final-product-requirements}

![][image1]  
![][image2]

![][image3]

Below is a representation of how the protocol will work starting from Digital Magazine Seller App to Buyer App and ONDC Network

![][image4]

[Link](https://www.figma.com/board/URRDHbA25hc3BBeagGWZuP/Magazines-Subscription?node-id=12-214&t=FP5Bd10Fs6OR6bS4-4)

ONDC aims to expand the networks’ offerings to include periodical subscription services from a diverse group of publications across India.

The purpose of this document is to detail an MVP for periodical subscription services for magazines/books/newspapers etc on ONDC, which will enable purchase of said services on the Open Network. The open network shall allow interoperability between multiple marketplaces/platforms and is destined to expand further in terms of participants, increasing the category of periodical subscription services for publications, and adding diverse use cases in the future.

This document is intended to be the requirements specification for any interested party to join the ONDC network as a participant under their chosen role(s).

Mode of Service delivery:

These are the primary modes to avail the Periodical Subscription Service:

1. Digital Subscription or online fulfilment : Which will be purchased through any buyer application. Digital content will be viewed by the user on the publication’s application or website
2. Print Subscriptions or offline fulfilment : Magazines will be delivered to the location chosen by the buyer (for example at the buyer’s home or in the office)

Both flows are covered as part of the MVP.

1. ## **In/Out of Scope** {#in/out-of-scope}

#

| Status  | Requirement \#                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Priority |
| ------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------- |
| **In**  | Purchase of a single magazine for both online consumption of content and offline delivery                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |          |
| **In**  | Purchase of subscription: Providing the feature to allow repeat orders on the base order using subscription based attributes such as duration of subscription, frequency. For eg. When a single magazine is purchased, it is the base purchase over which a subscription can be enabled by purchasing the same seller’s magazine for the next 6 months or in simpler terms subscribing to it. |          |
| **In**  | Status/track of subscription service: The buyer app will be able to track the status of the subscription as when the seller app provides the updates. Highlighting again, the delivery of content both online and offline is taken care by the seller app.                                                                                                                                    |          |
| **In**  | Cancellation: Cancellation of subscription through the protocol is possible                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |          |
| **In**  | Payment options for subscription: One shot payment, Auto EMI, Manual EMI                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |          |
| **Out** | Consumption of content on the buyer app: delivery of content both online and offline is taken care by the seller app only in phase 1                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |          |
| **Out** | Logistics on the network: Logistics services on network are not facilitated in this feature as of now.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |          |
| **Out** | Subscription pause: The buyer cannot pause the subscription on the buyer app as of now. However, they can always go back to the seller app for the same.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |          |
| **Out** | Subscription Renewal: The buyer cannot renew the subscription on the buyer app as of now. However, they can always go back to the seller app for the same.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |          |
| **Out** | Subscription Transfer: The buyer cannot transfer the subscription on the buyer app as of now. However, they can always go back to the seller app for the same.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |          |
| **Out** | Update to original order                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |          |

back with final quotation → Buyer makes the payment → Order is confirmed by the seller → Service is delivered by the seller to the buyer on the seller app | Main Path          | **Initiate Buyer’s Request** ![][image5] Buyer’s request for any print media product can be raised through the buyer app in three possible ways: Search by category: Category can be magazine. Other print media content are future use cases (newspapers, comics, books, articles) Search by city: Buyer app can raise a search request by city for eg. all sellers selling only in Lucknow Search by item: Let’s say the buyer wants to purchase Champak. The buyer app can raise an intent for search with this request also. For explanation purposes, search by category is defined here. Search by category Buyer on the buyer app raises an intent to purchase a print content of either of the following, Magazine Future use cases: Newspaper Comic Books articles The buyer can raise an intent of either one of the above or all of the above categories of print content available **Broadcast to Sellers** The interest is broadcasted to all the available sellers in the specific domain on the ONDC network via the gateway **Sellers Respond** Sellers will respond with their catalogues with variant attributes and other attributes for the buyer to define the discovery experience for the buyer. The variant attributes will be needed as selection from the buyer to define the quote of a purchasable item. The different attributes defined for the variant set are: Various category of periodicals available are magazine Future use cases: Newspaper Comic Books article Sellers can define the type of selling model available with them for every piece of content, this will be available as different type of purchase options in the catalogue, namely, Through fulfilment Subscription : Repeat delivery for both offline/online delivery of product Offline: Physical delivery Online: Digital delivery Through categories Paid Free Language: English, Hindi, Kannada etc. Edition: Edition of the magazine let’s say 5th edition or July edition Other attributes for sending the detailed catalogue for the buyer app to create the right experience for the buyer will be as below. Freebie offering : Other Inclusions such as newsletters, podcasts etc. These are considered 0 value items added to the base product File Size(optional): File size is used for defining the size of the product in case of online mode of fulfilment let’s say 87343 kb Publication Date: Date of publication of the magazine let’s say 27th May Number of pages of the magazine(optional): 100, 200, 300 etc. Volume number: Volume number of the magazine eg. volume 10, volume 8 Issue number: Issue number for the magazine Reading Age: Defines the optimal reading age for the content. Data type here is numeric therefore age as a number will be provided by the seller. Country of Origin(optional): Country where the content originated from India, Bangladesh Published/Marketed By: Defining who markets the product being purchased let’s say Living Media India Ltd. Downloadable: This is an information attribute where the seller informs the buyer through the buyer app that this print media content is available to be downloaded or not. Answering is the content available in downloaded format? YES/NO Preview: Quick read: Image based to create the nudge for buyer to purchase. This is where the seller can provide a preview of their content which can be used by the buyer before making the purchase. Rating: 1 star, 2 star, 3 star- Seller app can send across their rating for the particular magazine Genre: Health and Fitness, Lifestyle, Travel, Business, Finance , etc. Not limited to these values and the seller can send across the genre to support the product that they are offering. Base price for all products available Serviceability: The services of the seller may be limited to a city or a specific pincode or a set of pincodes. That needs to be defined for serviceability. It can also be PAN India. This is a Conditional mandatory attribute. For eg. if only offline magazine delivery is offered by the seller, this becomes a mandatory attribute else it’s optional. In case the seller provides subscription for any of the products, the subscription attributes also need to be sent along with the catalogue to facilitate the ~~buyer~~ app to create a subscription experience [(Refer Use Case 2\)](#use-case-2)  **Offer Management & Selection ![][image6]** Buyer will select the most suitable product that they deem fit for their usage from all seller Apps catalogue Different models to be present for selection as received in the catalogue sent by the seller. Scenario 1: **online fulfilment model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers online consumption of content for its purchased magazine and not offline delivery. In this case the online model will be selected where the buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection for the seller to provide a quote. This will include Model: Purchase/Free Product: Magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Fulfilment Type: Online Language in which the magazine is available Edition: Edition of the magazine let’s say 5th edition or July edition Pincode: Conditional mandatory (will be provided for offline model) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product selection if the chosen product for purchase is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) Scenario 2: **Offline model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers only delivery of magazines at the buyer’s address and not online consumption of content. In this case the offline model is selected and the buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection call for the seller to provide a quotation. This will include Model: Purchase/Free Product: Magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Fulfilment Type: Offline Language Edition: 4th edition, July edition Address of delivery GPS location Pincode The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product if the chosen product for subscription is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) Scenario 3: **Offline and Online Model Selection** In case the seller app provides both offline delivery and online consumption of content for a particular magazine, the selection will be as below Model: Purchase/Free Product: magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Product Type: Offline \+ Online Two variants have been defined for selection of product as of now. If the seller wants, more variants can be defined in the catalogue. For eg. let’s suppose publication date is another variant attribute for which the price of the magazine will change; the seller can in this case define another variant attribute. Language Edition: 4th edition, July edition Pincode: Optional(Will be provided for offline model) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the package if the chosen package for subscription is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) The next step would be to place the order and agree to the terms of agreement by both seller and buyer app Pass the user identifier along with the address while the order is being placed to the seller app Buyer can select free content and start consuming it on the seller app **Payment and Confirmation of Order ![][image7]** The buyer will make the payment to confirm the order Payment can have three scenarios: Entire payment to be made pre-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made before the order is placed. Entire payment to be made post-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made post the order is placed and magazine delivered Entire payment to be made on-fulfilment Payment can be collected by both the buyer and seller app Buyer app collecting payment: Buyer app will send the payment link to the buyer and collect payment Buyer app to send details for confirming order to the seller app depending on the method of payment Item chosen details according to the select call transaction ID User Identifier: Phone number or email Once confirmed from the seller app, the magazine purchase would be mapped to the user Seller app collecting payment: While the seller app sends the terms of agreement for the sale to go through, the seller app will also provide the payment link along with the cancellation terms The buyer will make payment through the same link and order ID would be generated by the seller app The seller app will pass the order ID to the buyer app Post this the buyer app will map the content to the user and save the same on the profile for the user **Post Order activities ![][image8]** Once the order is confirmed, the buyer and seller will take relevant actions as per the terms of the order Seller app magazine access availability to be visible to the user on Buyer Platform under the user profile section The content consumption will be happening on the seller app and the buyer app is only supposed to maintain the statuses related to the order. For this purpose a few statuses have been listed below which will be maintained on the buyer app as and when the status gets updated at the seller app’s end: Accepted: On order acceptance Completed: When the delivery of the order is completed In Progress: When the order is in progress In case the periodical is being delivered online/offline on different dates Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Digital Seller app which is taking care of delivery(both online and offline) of periodical, to respond with /on_status /on_status can have these statuses for fulfilment Pending Completed: When the purchase is complete By default, at the start of service, for all different dates status to be marked as Pending for fulfilment Buyer app to show the same status update to the user On the other hand, a user can also request for status of the magazine. In this case, buyer app to send a /status call and receive the /on_status from seller app to inform the user Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Print Seller app which is taking care of delivery(both online and offline) which is in this case is offline delivery of periodical, to respond with /on_status /on_status can have these statuses for fulfilment **Pending**: When the magazine is yet to be delivered **Packed**: Start of process of delivery of magazine where packaging takes place **Agent-Assigned**: Delivery partner assigned **Order-Picked-Up**: Picked up for delivery **Out-For-Delivery Completed**: Delivery completed By default, at the start of service, for all different dates status to be marked as Pending As and when actual delivery is completed for the periodical, /on_status to send completed to mark the delivery completion of a magazine On the other hand, a user can also request for status of the magazine. In this case, buyer app to send a /status call and receive the /on_status from seller app to inform the user |
| **Alternate Path** | If the seller app provides for subscription of magazine content, they can send across their catalogue for subscription as explained in use case 2 | Main Path          | **Thought ![][image9]** The seller is offering print subscription services and decides to send across the catalogue for ONDC enabled buyer app It identifies and formulates the catalogue such that it can be attributable to the subscription specific blocks and product details block Seller identifies that it has a print subscription for a magazine where weekly a new magazine can be delivered to the buyer and a newspaper subscription which can be delivered daily The seller identifies that associated attributes will be duration, frequency, fulfilment and product details for sending across all information needed for the buyer to plan the purchase Product 1: Magazine delivery on a weekly basis Duration: 1M, 3M, 6M, 12M Frequency: Weekly Fulfilment: Offline Serviceability: PAN India Product Details Category of periodical: Magazine Purchase model: Paid Number of pages: 25 Language: English Product 2: Newspaper delivery on a daily basis for a Mumbai based newspaper Duration: 1M, 3M, 6M, 12M Frequency: Daily Fulfilment: Offline Serviceability: PAN India Product Details Category of periodical: Newspaper Purchase model: Paid Edition: Mumbai Language: English Now when the buyer initiate’s a search request, the seller will send across this catalogue so that the buyer can take an informed decision and purchase a subscription **Initiate Buyer’s Request** Buyer’s request for any print media product can be raised through the buyer app in three possible ways: Search by category: Category can be magazine. Other print media content are future use cases (newspapers, comics, books, articles Search by city: Buyer app can raise a search request by city for eg. all sellers selling only in Lucknow Search by item: Let’s say the buyer wants to purchase Champak. The buyer app can raise an intent for search with this request also. For explanation purpose, search by category is defined here. **Broadcast to Sellers** The interest is broadcasted to all the available sellers on the ONDC network via the gateway **Sellers Respond The catalogue is being broken down into two blocks for explanation purposes: Subscription specific attributes and product details. Subscription specific attributes** Sellers can respond with their catalogues, with the following attributes Duration of subscription: The duration will be defined in the ISO format to enable a user to specify and answer- how long any particular subscription is needed for? P is the duration designator (for period) placed at the start of the duration representation. Y is the year designator that follows the value for the number of years. M is the month designator that follows the value for the number of months. W is the week designator that follows the value for the number of weeks. D is the day designator that follows the value for the number of days. T is the time designator that precedes the time components of the representation. 1 month duration can be presented as **P1M** 48 hours duration can be presented as **PT48H** 6 months duration can be presented as **P6M** Frequency of subscription: Defining the frequency at which the subscription needs to be delivered. Few possible frequencies for delivery for any fulfilment type can be: Daily Weekly Monthly Annually Example: Delivery of a magazine can be both weekly or monthly depending on the publisher **Product Details Catalogue** Sellers will respond with their catalogues, with the following attributes Various category of periodicals available are magazine Future use case: Newspaper Comic Books article Sellers can define the type of selling model available with them for every piece of content, this will be available as different type of purchase options in the catalogue Handled through fulfilment Subscription Offline: Physical magazine delivery Online: Content delivery is online Handled through categories Purchase of a single unit Free: Seller app needs to define that the payment in this case being collected from the buyer is 0 Base price for all packages available Freebie: Other Inclusions such as newsletters, podcasts etc. These are considered 0 value items added to the main product File Size(optional): File size is used for defining the size of the product in case of online mode of fulfilment let’s say 87343 kb Publication Date: Date of publication of the magazine let’s say 27th May Number of pages of the magazine(optional): 100, 200, 300, 400 Volume number: Volume number of the magazine eg. volume 10, volume 8 Issue number: Issue number for the magazine Language: English, Hindi, Kannada Reading Age: At what age and above is the content consumption is recommended for the buyer 18, 14+ Country of Origin(optional): Country where the content originated from India, Bangladesh Edition: Edition of the magazine let’s say 5th edition or July edition Published/Marketed By: Defining who markets the product being purchased let’s say Living Media India Ltd. Downloadable: Answering is the content available in downloaded format? YES/NO Preview: Quick read: Image based to create the nudge for buyer to purchase Rating: 1 start, 2 star, 3 star Genre: Health and Fitness, Lifestyle, Travel, Business, Finance , etc Serviceability: Conditional mandatory. For eg. if only offline magazine delivery is offered by the seller, this becomes a mandatory attribute else it’s optional. **Offer Management & Selection ![][image10]** Buyer will select the most suitable subscription that they deem fit for their usage from all seller Apps catalogue Different models to be present for selection as received in /on_search Scenario 1: **online fulfilment model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers online consumption of content for its purchased magazine and not offline delivery. In this case the online model will be selected where the buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection for the seller to provide a quote. This will include Model: Purchase/Free Product: Magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Fulfilment Type: Online Two variants have been defined for selection of product as of now. If the seller wants, more variants can be defined in the catalogue. For eg. let’s suppose publication date is another variant attribute for which the price of the magazine will change; the seller can in this case define another variant attribute. Language Edition: 4th edition, July edition Pincode: Conditional mandatory (will be provided for offline model) Duration of the subscription: 1 month, 6 month, annual subscription Frequency of the subscription: daily, weekly, monthly The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product selection if the chosen product for purchase is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) Scenario 2: **Offline model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers only delivery of magazines at the buyer’s address and not online consumption of content. In this case the offline model is selected and the buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection call for the seller to provide a quotation. This will include Model: Purchase/Free Product: Magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Fulfilment Type: Offline Language Edition: 4th edition, July edition Address of delivery GPS location The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product if the chosen product for subscription is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) Scenario 3: **Offline and Online Model Selection** In case the seller app provides both offline delivery and online consumption of content for a particular magazine, the selection will be as below Model: Purchase/Free Product: magazine Future use cases: Newspapers Books Comics Articles Product Type: Offline \+ Online Language Edition: 4th edition, July edition Pincode: Optional(Will be provided for offline model) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the package if the chosen package for subscription is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) The next step would be to place the order and agree to the terms of agreement by both seller and buyer app Pass the user identifier along with the address while the order is being placed to the seller app Buyer can select free content and start consuming it on the seller app **Payment and Confirmation of Order ![][image11]** The buyer will make the payment to confirm the order Payment can have three scenarios: Entire payment to be made pre-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made before the order is placed. For eg. the entire payment for the subscription needs to be made before confirming the order Entire payment to be made post-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made post the order is placed and magazine delivered. For eg. once the delivery of all magazines is done at the buyer’s residence Entire payment to be made on-fulfilment: As and when each magazine gets delivered, payment needs to be done Payment can be collected by both the buyer and seller app Buyer app collecting payment: Buyer app will send the payment link to the buyer and collect payment Buyer app to send details for confirming order to the seller app or mandate details depending on the method of payment Item chosen details according to the select call transaction ID Mandate registration details in case a mandate is registered User Identifier: Phone number or email Once confirmed from the seller app, the magazine purchase would be mapped to the user Later using the RSP mechanism on the network already in place, the buyer will send across the payment to the seller app Seller app collecting payment: There can be various methods of collecting payment in this case which are being facilitated on the protocol One shot payment: The entire payment of the subscription is being taken by the seller app in one go Mandate EMI: When the seller app gets a mandate registered for deducting payment at fixed intervals Manual EMI: Here the buyer will be manually paying at regular intervals to keep the subscription ongoing While the seller app sends the terms of agreement for the sale to go through, the seller app will also provide the payment link along with the cancellation terms in this case The buyer will make payment through the same link and order ID would be generated by the seller app The seller app will pass the order ID to the buyer app Post this the buyer app will map the content to the user and save the same on the profile for the user **Post Order activities ![][image12]** Once the order is confirmed, the buyer and seller will take relevant actions as per the terms of the order The content consumption will only happen at the seller app’s end. The buyer app has to maintain only the status of the order to provide the buyer an informed decision about the updates for his purchase Seller app magazine access to be visible to the user on Buyer Platform under the user profile section In case the periodical is being delivered online/offline on different dates, below scenarios are possible. Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Online Seller app which is taking care of delivery(both online and offline) of print content product, to update the buyer app for track of the subscription(/on_status) This call can have these statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: Subscription service is in progress Completed: When all the individual child orders have been delivered and order is completed Each fulfilment in an individual order can have the below listed statuses. For eg. let’s suppose a magazine needs to be delivered at the start of every month. In this case each month’s delivery of that one magazine out of many will be considered as one fulfilment. The statuses are: Pending Paused: Subscription paused on the seller app’s end Transferred: Subscription transferred from one user to another on the seller app Completed: Once the fulfilment is completed for delivery Buyer app to show the same status update to the user On the other hand, a user can also request for status of the product. In this case, buyer app to send a status call and receive the response to the status call from seller app to inform the user Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Offline Seller app which is taking care of delivery(both online and offline) which is in this case offline delivery of periodical, to update buyer app for keeping track of the subscription This call can have 3 statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: Subscription service is in progress Completed: When all the individual child orders have been delivered and order is completed As and when actual delivery is completed for all the magazines,seller app to send completed to mark the delivery completion of all magazines Each fulfilment in an individual order can have the below listed statuses. For eg. let’s suppose a magazine needs to be delivered at the start of every month. In this case each month’s delivery will be considered as one fulfilment. The statuses are: Pending Paused: Subscription paused on the seller app’s end Transferred: Subscription transferred from one user to another on the seller app Completed: Once the fulfilment is completed for delivery Cancelled: When the subscription is cancelled On the other hand, a user can also request for status of the product. In this case, buyer app to send a /status call and receive the /on_status from seller app to inform the user Cancellation updates would also be possible for subscriptions. Here the subscription will be cancelled on the consumption place ie. the seller app and will also be informed to the buyer on the buyer app |
| **Alternate Path** | In case the payment fails on the seller app, below use cases are possible in that case: Use case 1 \- Redirection and timed out When the seller app is collecting the payment and there happens to be a timeout error as the buyer failed to make the payment within the specified time limit: Buyer app would have not received a confirmation on the order In this case post completion of TAT for payment confirmation, seller app needs to do an unsolicited call to the buyer app informing about the error in payment Error: Payment Timed Out Post this the buyer app can reinitiate payment with the buyer(/init call) When the new payment is initiated by the buyer app, the seller app will generate a new payment link and sent across to the buyer app and reinitiation of order payment takes place Use case 2 \- Redirection and mandate setup failure When the seller app is collecting the payment and there happens to be a mandate setup failure: Buyer app would have not received a confirmation on the order In this case post completion of TAT for payment confirmation, seller app needs to do an unsolicited call to the buyer app informing about the error in payment Error: Mandate setup failure Post this the buyer app can reinitiate payment with the buyer(/in_it call) When the new payment is initiated by the buyer app, the seller app will generate a new payment link and sent across to the buyer app and reinitiation of order payment takes place Use case 3 \- Payment link not timed out but the buyer app makes a /Status call to the seller app When the seller app is collecting the payment and there happens to be a payment failure at the seller app’s end: Buyer app can make a status call to get the updated status of order Buyer app would have not received a confirmation on the order In this case, the buyer app will send a request to the seller app of not receiving a payment confirmation to which the seller app will inform back with an error: Error: Payment failure Or Error: Mandate setup failure Post this the buyer can reinitiate payment for the purchase by connecting with the buyer and restarting the payment process There will be other use cases, these are just a few examples. | **Alternate Path** | If there is a change in address at the time of order confirmation In this case when the buyer updates a different address than the GPS location captured by the buyer app, the buyer app can choose to restrict the user for not updating a different access The buyer app requests the seller app to confirm the order with the new address: The seller app can inform an error in this case when the new address is provided The buyer app can then reinitiate the process by taking a new address and then confirming the order ##

4.  ## **Future Features & International Expansion** {#future-features-&-international-expansion}

| Priority | Requirement                                                         | Comment |
| :------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------ | :------ |
| **1**    | Publication date/month selection by buyer for collectibles use case |         |
| **2**    | Transfer subscription on buyer app                                  |         |
| **3**    | Pause subscription on buyer app                                     |         |
| **4**    | Coupled subscription(AIM+India Today)                               |         |
| **5**    | Payment Method Updation                                             |         |
| **6**    | Offline downloading on buyer app                                    |         |
